United States Declares to Britain Maintenance of International Law Integrity, Also Sent Note to Britain Regarding the Confiscation of German Goods, US Merchant Ship Navigation Plan Under Study

London The American Chargé d'Affaires in Britain met with Foreign Office officials this afternoon and presented a note, declaring a reservation of all rights regarding Britain's blockade of German export trade. The British government will submit a reply after careful study. (Havas dispatch of the 8th)

Washington The United States has notified Britain that it is reserving its rights under international law due to the Allies' decision to confiscate German exports carried by neutral ships. The original text was published here today, stating that the tendency to disregard international law is threatening the security of peace-loving countries, and at this time, we must strive to uphold the integrity of international law. If Britain's order to confiscate German exports is implemented, American ships carrying goods produced or owned by Germany will be taken to British ports, regardless of the place of loading or unloading, and regardless of the ownership of the goods when the ship is intercepted. According to American legislation, American ships have been prohibited from operating in certain areas on the west coast of Europe, so the situation of interfering with American ships on the grounds of breaking the blockade should not occur. A belligerent country's plan for another belligerent country should not be appropriately extended to expand the belligerent country's rights over neutral ships, or to the extent that it hinders the legitimate trade of neutral countries. The United States cannot ignore the plans to be adopted by the British Order in Council, and if it is implemented, it will increase the many obstacles and damages that international trade is currently encountering. Diplomatic circles here, in view of the current political situation in the United States and the accusations of isolationists against the government's actions, believe that the wording of this American document could not be more moderate, but they also feel that the US government has failed to use harsher wording, because the United States has not protested against Germany's laying of mines or detaining ships. (Reuters dispatch of the 8th)

Washington After meeting with US Ambassador to Britain Kennedy yesterday, President Roosevelt stated at a reception for reporters that the government is currently studying a plan for the navigation of US merchant ships, so that US ships can sail outside the war zone, carrying goods currently carried by ships from the warring countries. The President also said that he would meet with Kennedy yesterday afternoon to discuss world affairs. The President has discussed with Kennedy a plan to restore the southern pine trade, which has been stalled due to the European blockade. Kennedy stated at a reception for reporters yesterday, "The United States will never participate in the European war." When a reporter asked if the Allies hoped for US assistance, Kennedy replied, "No one in the world loves war. If the United States adheres to neutrality, they cannot force it." (United Press dispatch of the 9th)

London Regarding Britain's blockade of German export trade, the US government has submitted a note declaring reservation of rights. British political and public opinion circles originally believed that Germany's submarine and mine warfare posed a major threat to international trade and the lives and property of the people of various neutral countries. Britain had no choice but to take legitimate self-defense measures. In view of the situation, the United States would not, after other neutral countries, make accusations against Britain. Now it is beyond expectations, and after being surprised, I feel quite depressed. Political figures also said that this issue is a matter of life and death in Britain. If it does not want to risk defeat or allow the war to drag on for a long time, it is inconvenient to sit idly by while Germany uses all means to fight, without trying to deal with it. For the benefit of various neutral countries, the two allied countries, Britain and France, must win before they can obtain protection. In short, this matter is a comparison between Sweden's blockade policy and the blockade policies of Britain and France. All neutral countries will be able to choose which side they want to win. Now that the United States has submitted a note, the British government should naturally provide an answer in law and try to reduce inconvenience in practice. (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

New York, Regarding the blockade of German export trade by Britain and France, after the US government submitted a note to Britain yesterday, reserving its rights, the New York Times commented, "The position of the United States has been explained by this note. In other words, the United States, as the most powerful neutral country, has always regarded maintaining international law as its main interest, but it also sympathizes with the efforts of Britain and France to curb German aggression. This is why the word 'protest' was not used in this note. It is hoped that Britain will do its best to ensure that the needs of the country and the interests of the United States do not run counter to each other. (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

British Warship Intercepts a German Ship

London The German ship "Oldenburg" (3,648 tons) was intercepted by a British warship in a certain sea area. (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

French War Report

Paris The General Headquarters has issued War Report No. 192, stating that today, outpost troops and artillery units of our enemy and our side have been slightly active in a certain place in Qianqian. (Havas dispatch of the 8th)

Paris The General Headquarters has issued War Report No. 193, stating that "infantry and artillery units of our enemy and our army were quite active in several places on the front line last night." (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

British Warship HMS Jersey Damaged by German Submarine, British Aircraft Sinks Three German Submarines, Several Ships of Various Countries Have Another Accident

London The British Admiralty announced today that the British destroyer "Jersey" (1,690 tons) was damaged by a torpedo from a German submarine on December 7. It has now entered the port, with two officers and eight sailors dead, and twelve sailors injured. (Reuters dispatch of the 9th)

London The Admiralty recently issued a message stating that the British destroyer "Jersey" (displacement of 1,690 tons) was hit by a torpedo launched by a German submarine on the sea yesterday and suffered damage. (Havas dispatch of the 8th)

London It was announced officially last night that the British destroyer "Jersey," which was damaged by a German submarine mine attack on Thursday, safely returned to a British port yesterday. Twelve crew members were injured and ten are missing. It is believed that all those missing must have died. "Jersey" is one of Britain's newest destroyers, belonging to the "Geoffrey" class, suitable for construction in mid-April of this year, with a crew of 183 people and a displacement of 1,690 tons. This is the fifth British warship damaged by the German army since the war began. (United Press dispatch of the 9th)

London The Aviation Department recently issued a message stating that a British aircraft spotted a German submarine sailing on the sea in the eastern sea area this morning, and immediately dropped many underwater bombs and sank it. (Havas dispatch of the 8th)

London It has been learned that a total of three German submarines were sunk by British aircraft yesterday alone, one of which was the one that used a torpedo to hit the British destroyer "Jersey." (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

Copenhagen The German naval speedboat "Odense" sank after accidentally hitting a German mine near Langgland Island in Denmark. Several ships of the country immediately sailed to the rescue. Five or six crew members are missing and have probably died. (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

Amsterdam The British ship "Millier," displacement 1,088 tons, accidentally hit a mine near the southeast coast of Britain today and sank within two minutes. All crew members have landed safely. (Haitong dispatch of the 8th)

Amsterdam The Belgian ship "Louis Seed" has probably sunk after running aground on the British coast. The Belgian ship "Adur," displacement 1,105 tons, sailing from Portugal to Britain, has sent out a distress signal. The ship ran aground near the French coast. (Haitong dispatch of the 9th)

Amsterdam According to inquiries made here, the British Royal Mail Company's 8,795-ton cargo ship "Nassau Soda" has sunk in the Atlantic Ocean. A total of 87 sailors were on board, of which 44 landed safely and the whereabouts of the remaining 43 are unknown. (Haitong dispatch of the 9th)

London The British cargo ship "Gores" hit a mine and sank on the eastern coast last night. The shipowner and eight crew members are missing, and the other seven have been rescued. Another British ship "Franton" was sunk by a German submarine using a torpedo on the western coast. The whereabouts of nine crew members are unknown, and four others have been rescued, but all have been injured. They have landed at a port in Central England and will be sent to the National Hospital for treatment. In addition, according to a telegram from the capital of Denmark, the coal carrier "Coscia" exploded and sank the day before yesterday evening. All 21 crew members have died. (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

Amsterdam The British cargo ship "Manchester Regiment" (6,000 tons) collided with the "Minister" in the Atlantic Ocean. The "Minister" immediately sank, and the "Manchester Regiment" also sank. The whereabouts of several crew members are unknown. The crew members of both ships arrived in Britain last night on another British ship. (Haitong dispatch of the 9th)

German Air Force Launches Large-Scale Raid on British Coast, Encounters British Air Force in Battle, Germany Boasts of Controlling the Skies Over the North Sea

London It was announced here last night that German aircraft attacked the Firth of Forth yesterday, one of the large-scale attacks on the British coast since the outbreak of the European war. After a fierce battle with British aircraft, they returned to their base with scars. One German aircraft was shot down and crashed into the sea. After the large-scale German attack, two British aircraft encountered two German aircraft near the Firth of Forth. The British aircraft drove the German aircraft westward, and one German aircraft was severely damaged. (United Press dispatch of the 9th)

Berlin The German official newspaper mentioned for the first time yesterday the "controlled flight" over the North Sea. A Haitong News Agency reporter learned from responsible sources that the "controlled flight" of the German Air Force has great significance. Germany will permanently control the area of the North Sea from the German coast to the Shetland Islands, 900 kilometers long and 450 to 100 kilometers wide, which has been controlled by the "elite troops" of the German Air Force. Germany has used the air hegemony of the North Sea to control the navigation of various ships. (Haitong dispatch of the 9th)

Paris According to news last night, several squadrons of German bombers penetrated deep into French territory on Thursday night, attempting to bomb Paris without success. German aircraft flew into French territory in clouds at an altitude of 23,000 feet and flew directly to Paris. They were immediately detected by the French army, and German aircraft were repelled by anti-aircraft artillery on the east side of Paris. Also, it was reported that the German army captured a large number of Polish guerrillas in Poland. The German authorities have dispatched 4 divisions of 60,000 people to the Qinghe River and the upper reaches of the Vistula River to suppress Polish guerrillas. (United Press dispatch of the 9th)

Third Batch of British Youth Called Up for Military Service

London 250,000 young men across the country, all between the ages of 20 and 23, reported to local conscription offices this morning, so that they could enlist for training at the end of this month. This is the third batch of British youth conscripted since the outbreak of the war. The previous two batches totaled 400,000 people. Combined with this batch, there are already 650,000 people. (Havas dispatch of the 9th)

Iraq Young King Seriously Ill

Cairo According to news from Baghdad, the King of Iraq, Faisal II, who is 5 years old, has become seriously ill. Diplomatic circles here express doubt, believing that the King of Iraq's serious illness is related to the activities of General Said. Said believes in a pro-British policy and has the ambition to become a dictator himself. (Haitong dispatch of the 9th)

Italy Adopts a Wait-and-See Policy on the European Situation, Especially Emphasizing Balkan Security; German-Italian Alliance Remains Unwavering; Ciano to Clarify Stance Next Saturday

Rome – The "Italian Daily" published an article by Mussolini's mouthpiece, Gaida, stating that the Italian state of "non-belligerence" mentioned in the Fascist Grand Council's communiqué differs from neutrality. Any involvement in the Balkan countries involves Italy's interests, which is why Italy pays special attention to developments in the Balkans. The communiqué reflects Italy's reserved attitude and confirms the steadfastness and continuation of Italian policy. German-Italian relations remain unchanged as stipulated in their alliance. It is expected that Foreign Minister Ciano will speak in parliament next week to elaborate on Italy's stance. (Reuters, 9th)

Rome – Foreign Minister Ciano is scheduled to deliver a speech to the Fascist Corporations Council on the 16th of this month, explaining Italy's current policy. According to reports, the Foreign Minister will present a clear and comprehensive report on Italy's policy at that time. Furthermore, various newspapers have commented on the communiqué issued by the Fascist Grand Council yesterday, stating that Italy attaches the utmost importance to maintaining the status quo in the Balkan Peninsula and the Danube region. The "Messenger" newspaper also stated, "Our country's policy towards the Balkan Peninsula is based on geography, history, economics, and even the European balance of power. In short, the Balkan Peninsula should belong to the Balkan nations." (Havas, 9th)

Paris – The communiqué issued by the Italian Fascist Grand Council yesterday has been commented on by the local morning newspapers, which generally believe that Italy's primary consideration of its own interests is its right and cannot be opposed by anyone. The country's current attitude remains ambiguous, but in fact, considering the course of this war, it is expected that the country would adopt such an attitude. The right-wing "Petit Parisien" newspaper stated, "No one is currently attempting to break the German-Italian axis. If this axis were to break one day, it would be Germany that did it. In other words, it would be because Germany wanted to threaten, destroy, or encompass everything, which has nothing to do with us." The moderate "L'Ordre" newspaper stated that Germany and Italy had once signed a secret agreement stipulating that if one signatory country went to war, the other must provide assistance in the army, navy, and air force. However, if Germany went to war before 1942, the year of the opening of the Rome International Exposition, Italy could temporarily not participate in the war. Foreign Minister Ciano visited Adolf Hitler in Germany on October 8th of this year to declare the country's decision to invoke this reservation clause and avoid joining the war, thus showing that Italy is not refusing to fulfill its obligations under the political and military agreement. In short, Italy's current policy is clearly a wait-and-see policy. The fact that the Fascist Grand Council's communiqué yesterday did not mention the Finnish incident is clear evidence of this. (Havas, 9th)

Uruguay Decides to Withdraw from the League

Uruguay’s Capital – The Uruguayan Senate, by a vote of 22 to 4, decided to withdraw from the League of Nations. Newspapers prominently featured speeches by senators criticizing the League, believing it had completely failed to guarantee peace and security. Foreign Minister Juan expressed strong opposition to the withdrawal and had attempted to prevent the Senate vote, arguing that a decision should be made after the League of Nations convenes and the attitudes of the various countries are known. Political figures therefore believe that the Senate's decision to withdraw is a failure of the government. Uruguay's note to the League of Nations aimed to expel the Soviet Union from the League, not for Uruguay itself to withdraw. (Haitong, 9th)

Philippine Hopes to Postpone Independence Deadline; President Quezon to Visit the U.S. Next Summer

Hong Kong International News Agency, Washington, 8th – According to information obtained by this agency, Philippine President Quezon plans to visit the United States next June to urge the U.S. to extend the date for the complete independence of the Philippines beyond the scheduled year of 1946. It is understood that Quezon intends to request the government to amend the Philippine Independence Act, so that the Philippines will not be absolutely independent de jure, but can obtain the status of a self-governing dominion de facto. Official sources say that from the U.S. government's point of view, the Philippine issue is still open to discussion, as the government has always regarded the Philippines as a major key to the U.S. maintaining its position in the Far East. According to reliable sources, U.S. High Commissioner to the Philippines Sayre has fully informed President Quezon of this intention, and has also told him that the issue of extending Philippine independence should be initiated by the Philippine side first. It is understood that Quezon's trip next year is due to the Philippine people's desire to maintain ties with the U.S., and because of the European and Asian situation, they hope to rely on U.S. military strength for protection. Official sources say that Japan's new policy aims to end the Sino-Japanese War as soon as possible and has proposed a non-aggression pact to the Soviet Union, which is causing great panic in the Philippines. Once the Japanese troops in China can be redeployed, the Philippines, located in a key position between Japan and the Dutch East Indies, which Japan covets, may be subject to the possibility of Japan using force to implement annexation. Official sources say that Philippine strategists, in order to ensure national security, seem to be prepared to implement the proposal to extend independence. According to sources in Washington, the Philippines, in view of Germany's annexation of Poland with lightning speed, is deeply concerned that if Japan launches a southward advance policy, it may also quickly annex the Philippines. It has also been learned that the Japanese Navy has conducted exercises twice this year off the east coast of New Guinea. (8th)

Manila – According to news from here today, U.S. High Commissioner to the Philippines Sayre is currently conducting a broad inspection of the Philippines. His automobile has traveled through more than three provinces, meeting with local leaders everywhere and inspecting indigenous troops. It is reported that Sayre will go to the Japanese area of the Philippines, Davao Province, tomorrow. After arriving there, Sayre plans to inspect the Japanese hemp cultivation industry and the Japanese way of life. (United Press, 9th)

U.S. Navy Reassigns Flag Officers

Washington – According to an announcement by the Navy Department, Admiral Bloch, Commander-in-Chief of the Navy, is scheduled to be reassigned to the position of Commander of the Fourteenth Naval District, Pearl Harbor, Hawaiian Islands, on January 6th next year. The vacancy will be filled by Admiral Yarnell, Commander of the Battle Fleet, and Rear Admiral Snyder will succeed him as Commander of the Battle Fleet. (Havas, 9th)

Washington – Landon, the Republican presidential candidate in 1936, held a formal meeting with President Roosevelt at the White House yesterday to discuss U.S. foreign policy. Some people regard this meeting as having great significance, as it is generally recalled that Landon has repeatedly supported Roosevelt whenever the government has taken major actions on foreign policy. It is also generally recalled that some Republican senators regard President Roosevelt's recognition of the Soviet Union as a major political issue, and the meeting may be related to President Roosevelt's refusal to recall the U.S. ambassador to Moscow or to meet with the two. When Landon left the White House, he claimed that he and the President only discussed foreign policy and that the conversation was "informal." He did not mention the message he sent on Thursday requesting President Roosevelt to announce whether he intended to run for a third term. (United Press, 9th)

Soviet-Mongolian-Japanese-“Manchukuo” Boundary Demarcation Conference Held in Chita

Moscow – The Soviet-Mongolian-Japanese-“Manchukuo” Mixed Commission, established in accordance with the Molotov-Togo Agreement for the purpose of demarcating the boundaries of the recent conflict zone between the Mongolian People's Republic and “Manchukuo,” was convened on December 7 in the Chita region under the chairmanship of Brigade Commander Podenov, representative of the Soviet government. After exchanging greetings and documentary evidence, it has begun to discuss formal working procedures. (TASS, 9th)

Japan Seeks to Improve Relations with the Soviet Union

Tokyo – Although there is much discussion about Japan's intention to negotiate a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union, the general opinion here is that this is not entirely impossible, but it must wait until (1) some pending issues such as the rights of Japanese people in Northern Sakhalin and Japanese fishing issues are resolved, and (2) the Japanese-Soviet trade negotiations are established before negotiations can proceed. The "Nichi Nichi Shimbun" stated in its editorial today that the date for the formal opening of the trade negotiations has been tentatively set for mid-January next year. Japanese Ambassador to the Soviet Union Togo is currently having frank talks with Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov in the hope of facilitating the trade negotiations and obtaining a political solution to Japanese-Soviet relations. The Japanese government's commencement of trade negotiations with the Soviet Union before the Japanese-American trade negotiations are abolished clearly has deep meaning. Will Japan actively use the policy of controlling one country with another? (Reuters, 9th)

Japanese Prime Minister Meets with National Representatives

Tokyo – According to today's "Yomiuri Shimbun," Prime Minister Abe will meet with sixteen leaders of the "Spiritual Mobilization" to hear their reports on the public's reaction to government policies and to learn what measures they want the authorities to take. Among these sixteen people is Hatta, the former Minister of Commerce and Industry, who went to several districts from September to November to listen to the opinions of rural leaders. He learned that the people are now unanimously demanding the elimination of social ills, the cessation of the habit of exchanging gifts, and striving for simple clothing. On the last point, the people feel that government officials and the rich should set an example. Regarding government policies, the people demand a unified approach to the continued war in China and the situation around the world. Of the nine counties he visited, the people wanted the government to clarify its foreign policy so that the public would not be confused. As for the people's emotions towards the countries concerned, they varied greatly, with some advocating friendship with the Soviet Union and the United Kingdom, and others opposing it. (Reuters, 9th)

Two Instances of Valor by French Air Force Personnel

Paris – A Havas correspondent who witnessed the heroic actions of French air force personnel on the Eastern Front has selected the two most admirable and decisive achievements and described them as follows: According to reports, four air force personnel, including one reconnaissance officer, one pilot, and two machine gunners, recently boarded a large reconnaissance plane and went to reconnoiter the enemy. As soon as they arrived over the enemy's position, they were confronted by six Messerschmitt fighter planes. A fierce battle immediately broke out between the two sides. The French machine gunners calmly responded and at one point repelled the enemy planes, but soon the enemy planes returned and fired intensively at the reconnaissance plane with machine guns. The fuselage and wings were riddled with bullets. Finally, the enemy used incendiary bombs and hit the plane's left engine, which immediately caught fire. The plane suddenly descended from a height of 6,000 meters to 2,000 meters. At that time, the reconnaissance officer and one of the machine gunners had already been shot and killed. The other machine gunner was ordered by the pilot to jump with a parachute, but according to various reports, this person also failed to land safely. The pilot himself was injured, but he still flew the plane back to French territory. The plane finally landed not far from the front line, and the pilot died. According to the French Air Force authorities, the photos and other documents taken by the plane did not fall into the hands of the enemy. This is all due to the pilot's loyalty and dedication. In addition, another reconnaissance plane, after taking many photos, was surrounded by a squadron of enemy planes. The reconnaissance plane ascended and hid in the clouds, and fired at the enemy planes with machine guns. It then hurriedly flew back to its base, but the enemy planes closely pursued, firing intensively at it along the way. The reconnaissance plane's two machine gunners were both seriously injured and the machine guns were also damaged, so that it had no ability to fight back. At that time, the situation was already bordering on despair, but the pilot's improvisation allowed him to safely return to the base. However, all personnel were injured when they got off the plane and were immediately taken to the hospital for treatment. The heroic situation can be seen. (Havas, 8th)

Swiss Capital – German radio recently broadcast the news that the Romanian cargo ship "Durdub" carrying a large quantity of grain from the port of Constanța to Palestine has sunk in the Black Sea for unknown reasons. The whereabouts of the twelve crew members are unknown. (Havas, 8th)

"Sao Dang Bao" Warns the United States

Chongqing's "Sao Dang Bao" today commented on the losses suffered by Americans since the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese War due to Japanese bombing. The newspaper continued, saying that 50% to 60% of the losses suffered by American people and property in China at the hands of the Japanese were caused by weapons that the United States supplied to Japan. Now, Nomura is once again using sweet words with Grew, saying that Japan does not want to harm American rights and interests, but in fact, American lives and property are not guaranteed at all. Nomura's claim that Japan can guarantee that such incidents will not happen again is an empty check, because the Japanese government has never been able to keep its word, and even if the government hopes to keep its word, its soldiers in China will definitely not put the government in their eyes. In short, Nomura will definitely have no control over the military, so Grew and the American authorities should definitely not be deceived by what Nomura says. (United Press, 9th)

Chongqing today issued a statement describing the bombing of American industries in China by Japanese aircraft. It is said that since the outbreak of war between China and Japan over the Lugouqiao Incident and up to September of this year, a total of 36 American churches and schools have been bombed, resulting in 24 deaths and 25 injuries. (It is believed that this number includes both Americans and Chinese.) American properties destroyed by Japanese bombers also include the gunboat Panay and one aircraft of the China National Aviation Corporation, namely the Guilin. According to estimates by the Chinese official news agency, American properties have been bombed by Japanese aircraft a total of 150 times. (Reuters, 9th)

National Government Orders Praise for Wu Peifu

Chongqing National Government Order of the 9th: (1) Wu Peifu is to be posthumously awarded the rank of General of the First Class of the Army. This order, (2) The late Army General Wu Peifu was upright in character and steadfast in his aspirations. In the past, he reorganized the army and achieved remarkable fame. He hated evil and expelled the wicked, maintained righteousness and was incorruptible, which was beneficial to the world and people's hearts. Since the Mukden Incident, he has been concerned about national difficulties and has always encouraged himself with utmost loyalty. After the fall of Peiping, his situation became more difficult, but he was able to maintain his position from beginning to end, adding glory to the country and nation. His heroic demeanor and noble character were admired by both Chinese and foreigners. It was hoped that he would enjoy a long life and be a model for others. However, he passed away due to a minor illness, and in memory of his loyalty and righteousness, we express our deepest sorrow. He should be publicly praised, and the Military Affairs Commission should deliberate on generous condolences. A special funeral fee of 10,000 yuan is granted. His life story should be recorded and sent to the Historical Archives to show the state's concern for virtuous and upright people and to encourage utmost loyalty and righteousness. This order.

After the death of General Wu Peifu, the Chinese newspapers under Japanese control in Peiping expressed great praise for Wu, and the Japanese military spokesman also spoke to express his admiration, calling Wu the most capable and upright figure among Chinese soldiers, and saying that Wu's death was a great loss to Japan. He also said that Wu had expressed his willingness to assist the Japanese before his death, but the spokesman could not say to whom Wu had made this statement. Currently, Qi Xieyuan, Wang Yitang, Chen Zhongfu, and others are preparing for funeral affairs. The Peiping authorities have ordered all agencies to fly flags at half-mast on the third day of Wu's death and plan to hold a meeting to discuss the funeral ceremony. Wu's family has received numerous condolence telegrams and letters. Japanese dignitaries such as Konoe have also sent telegrams of condolence. Wu's coffin is temporarily placed in his residence in Dongcheng and is scheduled to be buried on the seventh day. It will be moved to Changchun Temple, and after the arrangements are completed, it will be buried in Penglai, Shandong Province. (9th)

Although the Japanese military in Peiping has released He Yingqin's condolence telegram to Wu Peifu's family to the press, Wu's family has not received this telegram. According to Chinese reports, Jin Yunpeng, the former Premier of the Anfu Clique, arrived in Peiping from Tianjin today. The Japanese military may give Jin the position previously given to Wu Peifu. (United Press, 9th)

Civil Service Performance Appraisal Regulations

Chongqing (Continued from yesterday) Article 6. Civil service performance appraisals shall be divided into preliminary review and review. The heads of each agency shall designate a number of senior officials to form a performance appraisal committee, with one person as chairman, to conduct the preliminary review. The heads of agencies shall conduct the review. However, if the head of the agency has only one rank or the agency is in a war zone and cannot form a performance appraisal committee, the appraisal may be conducted directly by the head. The performance appraisal committee shall conduct the preliminary review, taking into account the opinions of the directly superior officers of the persons being appraised, comparing the performance of all persons being appraised in the agency, and based on the usual records and rewards and punishments, assess the scores in the performance appraisal form and report them to the senior officer for review to determine rewards and punishments. After the performance appraisal form is reviewed by the senior officer, it shall be compiled and sealed in accordance with its official rank, and sent to the examination and appointment agency for verification and registration. The form of the performance appraisal form shall be determined separately. Article 7. If a civil servant should be promoted due to performance appraisal but has no rank to be promoted to, the following provisions shall apply: (1) If the person has already been promoted to the highest rank of recommendation or appointment, and the rank is high and the salary is low, a certificate of commendation shall be given or the salary shall be appropriately increased. If the salary has reached the highest amount, a record of recommendation or treatment may be given, but only if the person has been in the highest rank of recommendation or appointment for more than three years. If the person has been in the highest rank for less than three years, a certificate of commendation shall be given instead. (2) If the person has already been promoted to the highest rank of his position, and the rank is high and the salary is low, a certificate of commendation shall be given or the salary shall be appropriately increased. If the salary has reached the highest amount of the position, a record of promotion may be given. The form of the certificate of commendation shall be determined separately. Article 8. If a civil servant should be demoted due to performance appraisal but has no rank to be demoted to, the salary shall be reduced in proportion to the number of ranks. Article 9. If a civil servant has one of the following situations and the total score in the performance appraisal is 80 or more, a certificate of commendation shall be given: (1) The probationary staff member is changed to a substantive appointment and has been promoted to the grade until the performance appraisal for less than one year. (2) The position has been changed and has been promoted to the grade until the performance appraisal for less than one year. (3) In accordance with Articles 9 and 10 of the Measures for the Group Meetings of Party, Government, and Military Agencies and the Guidance of Public and Private Life Behavior, the grade has been promoted before the performance appraisal is held. Article 10. If a civil servant has continued to hold his current position for more than five years and the total score of three performance appraisals is 80 or more, the Ministry of Examination may be requested by the Ministry of Personnel to give a medal. The regulations for awarding medals shall be determined by the Examination Yuan. Article 11. For personnel serving in the war zone who can complete the work related to the direct war of resistance in accordance with the tasks and achieve outstanding performance, in addition to giving rewards in accordance with this Ordinance, they may also be awarded the Courageous Medal in accordance with the Ordinance for the Award of Medals. Article 12. The agencies for handling civil service performance appraisals shall be divided according to the following provisions: A. Handled by the Ministry of Personnel: (1) Civil servants in the central ministries, committees, departments, and offices, and their directly subordinate agencies inside and outside the capital. (2) Civil servants in the provincial governments and their subordinate departments, offices, and bureaus. (3) Civil servants in the municipal governments subordinate to the Executive Yuan and the municipal governments subordinate to the provincial governments, and their subordinate departments, offices, and bureaus. (4) Civil servants in courts at all levels. (5) Civil servants in the administrative inspectorate offices of the provinces. (6) County magistrates of each province. (7) Civil servants in the administrative district management offices and civil servants appointed by the provinces. B. Handled by the Personnel Trust Review Committee: (1) Civil servants in the provincial governments and the county sub-agencies under the departments, offices, and bureaus. (2) Civil servants in the administrative inspectorate offices and their subordinate agencies. (3) Civil servants in the county governments, offices for setting up bureaus, and their subordinate agencies. Civil servants appointed by the provinces. After the Personnel Trust Review Committee handles the performance appraisal, it shall prepare a table and report it to the Ministry of Personnel for record. Article 13. If the Ministry of Personnel believes that there is any doubt about the performance appraisal scores or rewards and punishments of civil servants, it may send personnel to verify it or notify the agency to describe the facts in detail or provide conclusive evidence. Article 14. After the performance appraisal rewards and punishments of civil servants are approved by the Ministry of Personnel, the agency shall be notified to implement them separately. Article 15. If a civil servant who has passed the performance appraisal leaves his job, he may request the original agency to transfer to the original performance appraisal agency to issue a performance appraisal certificate of qualification. The form of the performance appraisal certificate of qualification shall be determined separately. Article 16. Personnel handling performance appraisals shall strictly keep secrets and shall not engage in favoritism or fraud, or omissions or errors. Violators shall be punished separately in accordance with the law. Article 17. For personnel appointed, assigned, or permitted to be employed by various agencies, and other personnel whose performance appraisal is not applicable to this Ordinance, the competent officers may refer to the provisions of this Ordinance and give appropriate performance assessments. Article 18. This Ordinance shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (9th)

The Concession Authorities Set a Rice Price Limit, Strictly Enforced Starting Today, with the Highest Grade White Rice at Forty-Five Yuan Per Shi, and Xian Rice Priced at Thirty-Eight Yuan Per Shi; Violators Will Be Reported to the Public Works Department for Punishment

The concession authorities of both concessions are quite concerned about the entire rice market in Shanghai. Given the rising rice prices, which are greatly related to the security within the concessions, it is heard that the Public Works Department of the Public Concession is preparing legal sanctions. Mr. Hoteck Quy, the Deputy General Manager of the department, specifically telegraphed Mr. Fu Qian Geng, the Director of the Rice Shop Tea Association Market Management Committee, and Mr. Zhang Nian Xuan, the Chairman of the Rice Merchants Association, at 2:00 PM yesterday. After receiving the telegram, Mr. Fu and Mr. Zhang rushed to the department to meet with Mr. Hoteck. Mr. Fu and Mr. Zhang separately reported on the recent situation of the rice market, the source of rice, the chaotic situation of the market, and the strict supervision of the transactions of fellow traders in the market. Mr. Hoteck immediately discussed the selling price of rice: (1) the highest price for white rice should be forty-five yuan per shi (one market shi is 160 catties), and (2) the price for Xian rice should be thirty-eight yuan per shi, and no one should take advantage of the situation to raise prices, in order to maintain the entire rice market within the concessions. Anyone exceeding this price limit will be reported to the authorities for severe punishment.

Soybean and Rice Association Holds Emergency Meeting

In addition to instructing the Rice Shop Association Market Management Committee to take strict measures to ban illegal cross-level transactions in the market, the Shanghai Soybean and Rice Trade Association also convened the 57th joint meeting of the 3rd Executive and Supervisory Committee at 3:00 PM yesterday at the Miscellaneous Grain and Oilcake Exchange on the second floor of 15 Avenue Edward VII. Seventeen committee members attended, including Xing Zhi Gang, Chen Zi Yi, Zhu Zi Xiang, She Bing Wen, Jin Zhao Yun, Hu Wen An, Cha Sheng Ming, Fu Qian Geng, Yin Fu Xiang, Xu Ye Sun, Zhou Zhi Zhen, Gu Yi Sheng, Zhang Nian Xuan, Zhu Xiang Sheng, Jiang Hong Bin, Yan Xiao Quan, and Zhang Li Zhong. Xing Zhi Gang, the chairman, first reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by Fu Qian Geng reporting on his meeting with the authorities and the chaotic situation of the rice market. Chen Zi Yi then contributed his opinions on comprehensive solutions. The discussion then began and concluded at 8:00 PM.

Planning for Comprehensive Solutions

One motion was discussed yesterday: The recent increase in rice prices is causing hardship for the common people and affecting local security. How should we find ways to remedy this situation and achieve balance? Upon investigation, the recent increase in rice prices is a cause for concern. We should find ways to remedy this situation and achieve balance. The association, recognizing the importance of this matter, convened a meeting for serious discussion and believes that there are three short-term solutions: (1) Accept the Public Works Department's intention to temporarily set the price of high-grade white rice at no more than forty-five yuan per shi, and foreign rice and Ke Xian rice at no more than thirty-eight yuan per shi, with Du Xian and Yang Xian rice excluded from this rule. This will be announced and implemented from the 10th of this month, and the Management Committee will strictly enforce it. Violators will be reported to the concession authorities for punishment. (2) The agreement reached in the rice market yesterday to set a three-day deadline for the delivery of domestic rice is a good policy and should be ratified, but it should be supplemented to ensure that all domestic rice, Xian rice, and foreign rice are delivered within three days of the transaction. Violators should be severely punished. (3) Please report any unscrupulous merchants who are manipulating the market and hoarding goods as much as possible. The association will forward the reports to the concession authorities for severe punishment. There are also three long-term solutions: (1) From yesterday onwards, all rice, wheat, and miscellaneous grains transported to the port by train should not be allowed to be transported to the concessions. We should immediately write to the concession authorities to find a way to dredge the canal to alleviate the urgent need. Also, the price of Wuhu rice is only a little over fifteen yuan at most. We should immediately write to the concession authorities to find a way to obtain 50,000 bags of Wuhu Xian rice export permits for merchants to use, thereby increasing the source. The price can be set by the concession authorities according to the cost. (2) It is suggested that the concession authorities, the Chamber of Commerce, and Yu Qia Qing convene a meeting of various public organizations to discuss group purchases of foreign rice to increase strength and add sources. Please also ask the Chamber of Commerce to inform the banking industry to provide loans as much as possible to those who purchase domestic or foreign rice. (3) Please ask the Chamber of Commerce and Yu Qia Qing to forward a request to the Ministry of Finance, following the previous example, to apply for legal foreign exchange, at least to order 50,000 bags of foreign rice to be used for price stabilization and to help the poor.

Actively Negotiating Second Price Stabilization Effort

Yu Qia Qing had previously initiated a group purchase of Saigon foreign rice, entrusted to the Accountants Association for registration, and this association, together with the Shanghai Refugee Relief Association and other organizations, organized the first price stabilization effort. Although it was a drop in the bucket and did not solve the problem, many people went to buy miscellaneous goods. This time, the source of rice has not been interrupted, but the price of rice has continued to rise, breaking the new record of forty-eight yuan. The Soybean and Rice Trade Association, recognizing this, had Zhang Nian Xuan contact Yu Qia Qing to discuss a second Saigon rice price stabilization effort. Recognizing the importance of this matter, it was determined that it could not be achieved in the short term. Currently, all parties are actively negotiating, and once everything is in order, it will be categorized and processed step by step.

The Rice Shop Tea Association Market Management Committee agreed the day before yesterday that the delivery of goods after transactions among fellow traders in the market should be limited to three days for the time being. Whether it is customer selling to shop, shop selling to firm, or firm selling to shop, all must comply and allow for actual transactions and must not engage in empty sales. The punishment methods include suspending business for minor violations and requesting the General Association to revoke membership for major violations. The notice was issued to the market and sent to more than one hundred firms yesterday morning. It is learned that the committee has scheduled its 56th committee meeting at the public sampling office in the market at 10:00 AM this morning. At that time, the price limits of forty-five yuan for the highest grade white rice and thirty-eight yuan for foreign rice and Ke Xian rice will be reported, and all rice trading firms will be strongly urged to comply, in order to stabilize the entire rice market. The Soybean and Rice Trade Association decided to issue a public notice to the market this morning to implement it.

Large Numbers of Japanese and Puppet Troops Transferred to Shanghai, More Than Nine Thousand Arrived on the 7th and 8th, Most of the Houses in Nanshi Occupied

Between the 7th and 8th, a large number of troops from Taiwan and Manchukuo, totaling more than nine thousand, suddenly arrived in the Nanshi area. They were stationed in various locations in Nanshi, including Longmen Village on Penglai Road and Wu Li Street, the workers' children's school of the China Products Electric Company in front of the New Puyutang on Guohuo Road, the Hunan Guild Hall and Huining Guild Hall on Xiejiao Manufacturing Bureau Road, and the Nanputuo Road area south of Dapu Bridge. The troops were transferred from Wuhu, with disorganized uniforms and lacking winter clothing. At 8:00 PM on the night of the 7th, three soldiers from the puppet Manchukuo army broke into a civilian house near the puppet police station outside the Dananmen gate in Nanshi, searching for winter quilts. When the elderly occupant refused, they were enraged and stabbed him to death with a bayonet. After the arrival of these troops, the residents of Nanshi were terrified, fearing for their safety and discussing ways to protect themselves. Young men and women were particularly alarmed. It is also learned that the Shangchuan Guild Hall in Dongjiadu, Nanshi, and several newly built Western-style civilian houses at the former site of the police headquarters on Xundao Street inside Dadongmen are spacious and were not destroyed in the war. They have now been furnished with low beds and are prepared to house large numbers of Japanese troops who are being transferred to Shanghai. It is said that the total number of Japanese troops being transferred to Shanghai is in the tens of thousands and that they will all arrive by the 15th of this month. In addition to Nanshi, a similar number of troops, more than three thousand, arrived in the Hongkou area on the previous two days.

A large number of new notes have been exchanged by the Central, China, and Communications Banks, so the panic over one-yuan notes is no longer a problem. Chinese Insurance Industry Adjusts Fire Insurance

Adopting Gross and Net Prices, To Be Implemented Within Half a Year

Chinese fire insurance has always used gross price rates. This system is inconvenient for both policyholders and companies and needs to be adjusted. The Shanghai Insurance Trade Association, recognizing this, has resolved to change it to net prices, to be implemented within six months. Before the net price method is implemented, the discount rate will be slightly adjusted from today to ensure that the entire Chinese insurance industry can move forward in unison. Yesterday, a notice was sent to all Chinese and foreign insurance companies in the city, stating that from the 9th of October this year, all member companies of the association that underwrite various fire insurance policies for Chinese-owned properties in the city must adhere to a minimum discount rate of 18% of the price set by the association and may not give any other discounts or rebates. This notice is hereby given.

Uniformed Debt of Two Public Bonds Were Redeemed by Lottery Yesterday A Total of 2,380,000 Yuan Was Redeemed Electrical Debt Will Be Unified by the End of This Month and the Beginning of Next Year

The eighth redemption of principal of the 1936 Unified Public Debt Class E Bonds and the seventeenth redemption of principal of the 1935 Electrical Administration Public Debt were held yesterday morning at 10 o'clock. Fan Jietang from the National Debt Fund Management Committee, Pei Yunqing from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Shen Laiqing from the Bankers Association, Shen Jingliang from the Money Trade Association, Wang Lin from the Central Bank, Tang Yusun from the Bank of China, and Fan Chuchen from the Bank of Communications attended. The details are as follows.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Pei Yunqing reported that today is the eighth redemption of principal of the 1936 Unified Public Debt Class E Bonds and the seventeenth redemption of principal of the 1935 Electrical Administration Public Debt. The lottery method for the Unified Public Debt uses the last three digits, and the lottery method for the Electrical Administration Public Debt uses the last two digits. I will briefly report on the circumstances of the above public debts to everyone. The Unified Public Debt Class E Bonds were issued in February 1936, with a fixed amount of 260 million yuan. This is the eighth redemption of principal, with eight draws, each draw worth 260,000 yuan, for a total of 2,080,000 yuan. The 1935 Electrical Administration Public Debt was issued in October 1935, with a fixed amount of 10 million yuan. This is the seventeenth redemption of principal, with three draws, each draw worth 100,000 yuan, for a total of 300,000 yuan. The payment of principal and accrued interest for the Electrical Administration Public Debt lottery winners will begin on December 31, 1939, and will be paid by the Central, China, and Communications Banks in various locations. The payment of principal and accrued interest for the Unified Public Debt lottery winners will begin on January 31, 1940, in accordance with the procedures prescribed by the Ministry of Finance, and will be paid by the Central Bank and its authorized China and Communications Banks and the Central Trust Bureau in various locations. Now, I would like to ask the supervisors to check the lottery tickets and the ledger for accuracy before executing the lottery.

Winning Numbers

After the supervisors checked the lottery tickets and the ledger for accuracy, representatives from the Central, China, and Communications Banks executed the lottery. The winning numbers are listed below. (1) Unified Public Debt, eight draws: No. 033, No. 129, No. 281, No. 393, No. 676, No. 775, No. 831, No. 936. (2) Electrical Administration Public Debt, three draws: No. 20, No. 74, No. 83. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned from banking circles yesterday that the eighth redemption of principal and payment of interest for the five types of Unified Public Debt (A, B, C, D, and E) will begin at the end of January next year, but the specific procedures will be announced by the Ministry at that time. The seventeenth redemption of principal and payment of interest for the Electrical Administration Public Debt is scheduled to begin on the 31st of this month, but due to the interception of international telegraph fees, which serve as collateral, it is feared that the payment of principal and interest due this time will continue to be delayed.

Half Reduction of Taxes in Guerrilla Areas

Rent Should Also Be Reduced, Occupied Areas Exempted

The Executive Yuan has promulgated measures for the reduction and exemption of wartime taxes and rents and for the relief of abandoned farmland. It has already ordered the provincial governments to comply and implement them. The original text is as follows: Article 1: The reduction and exemption of land taxes and rents in war zones and the relief of abandoned farmland shall be governed by these measures. Article 2: War zones as referred to in these measures shall mean the following types of areas: (A) areas that have already fallen and are controlled by the Japanese; (B) areas in occupied places that have been recovered or are controlled by our guerrilla forces and can exercise political power; (C) areas close to the war zone and about to become battlefields. The various types of areas mentioned above and their scope shall be determined by the provincial government. Article 3: Land taxes in Type A areas shall be temporarily exempted. Article 4: Land taxes and surcharges in Type B areas should be reduced so that they do not exceed 50% of the original tax amount. Article 5: Rents in Type B areas should be reduced. The rent payable by the lessee shall not exceed two-thirds of the original rent amount. When a Type A area becomes a Type B area, its rent shall be governed by the provisions of the preceding paragraph. Article 6: The reduction of land taxes and rents in Type C areas shall be governed by the provisions of Articles 4 and 5 of these measures. Article 7: Land taxes in Type B and Type C areas may be converted into agricultural products based on market prices for payment. Article 8: If the owner of farmland in Type B and Type C areas has left his hometown and no one is managing it, the town and township office (joint security office) may manage it on his behalf, collect rent, pay taxes on his behalf, and collect a management fee from the balance of the managed property, but it shall not exceed 20% of the balance of the managed property. The rent that should be collected, the taxes that should be paid, the balance of the managed property, and the management fees collected for the farmland under the aforementioned entrusted management shall be reported to the county government for record. Article 9: If the farmland in the preceding article is not cultivated by anyone, the township office (joint security office) may temporarily designate local farmers to cultivate it, collect rent on behalf of the owner in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article, pay taxes on his behalf, and collect a management fee from the balance of the managed property. Article 10: Family members of soldiers fighting in the war of resistance shall have priority in renting the farmland in the preceding article. If the land of soldiers fighting in the war of resistance cannot be cultivated because there are no able-bodied men, the county government may designate local farmers to cultivate it on their behalf. The harvest from the cultivated land, after paying the rent, shall be divided equally between the cultivating farmers and the family members of the soldiers fighting in the war of resistance. Article 11: The implementing rules of these measures shall be formulated by the provincial governments and submitted to the Executive Yuan and the Military Affairs Commission for promulgation and implementation respectively, and shall be abolished when the war of resistance ends.

Shame and Integrity Movement Holds Meeting, Sends Condolences to Wu Peifu's Family

The Shanghai Shame and Integrity Movement Committee believes that General Wu Ziyu was in an adverse environment, but was not tempted by profit or intimidated by power. He supported the Party and the country and was unswervingly loyal. Now that he has passed away due to tooth disease, the committee expresses its deep condolences and sends a telegram to General Wu's family to express its condolences. The telegram reads: "To the family of General Wu Ziyu in Beiping, greetings. Mr. Ziyu once held a military seal and had the demeanor of a Confucian general. He then hid in the mountains and forests, resolute in his ambition as a man. With tigers and wolves pressing in, he was not intimidated by force. With foxes and rats running rampant, he was able to maintain his purity and resist vulgarity. He was the righteousness of the country and a model for the people. Suddenly hearing the news of his death, the cause of death is quite suspicious. Looking forward to the smoke and dust, the living must be more inspired. We offer our condolences and hope you will restrain your grief. Shanghai Shame and Integrity Movement Committee seal."

All Circles Initiate the Construction of a Bronze Statue

After General Wu Ziyu, a famous Chinese Confucian general and veteran, passed away in Ping on the 4th of this month due to a tooth disease, the news spread and the whole country mourned. The Supreme National Defense Council believes that Wu has been in the enemy's atmosphere for several years, but he has remained unblemished, strictly rejected inducements and threats, and maintained his integrity in his later years, demonstrating his righteousness. Therefore, he was posthumously awarded the rank of first-class general, and the National Government issued an order to commend him in order to encourage and motivate. "This autumn, all circles in the city also believe that General Wu's loyalty is outstanding and his righteousness is awe-inspiring, which is not only enough to make the crowd ashamed, but also the national righteousness is relied upon to flourish. His great personality is enough to leave a fragrance in history and last forever. In today's atmosphere of demonism, if there is no commemoration of Wu, there will be no way to commemorate the sages and warn the unworthy. Therefore, it was decided to initiate the fundraising for a bronze statue of General Wu. However, due to the special environment in Shanghai, a committee will not be established for the time being. It was decided to first conduct fundraising separately, requesting major newspapers to temporarily collect the donations. After raising a considerable amount, the method of building the bronze statue will be discussed, or the proposal will be suggested to the central government for adoption, and the donations will be remitted to Chongqing to comfort the heroic spirit and last forever."

Jianghai Customs Engineer Is Chopped

Sent to Lester Chinese Hospital for Treatment, Injuries Are Very Serious

Cornish, a British man residing in Room 104, Apartment 704, Jing'an Temple Road, is 41 years old and works as a mechanical engineer at the Jianghai Customs. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, at the Customs engine room in Lujiazui, Pudong, Cornish had a conflict with the coppersmith in the engine room due to a minor matter. Cornish was chopped in the head with an axe by the worker, and blood gushed out, causing him to faint. Afterwards, he was escorted by someone to take a small steamer to Puxi and taken by car to Lester Chinese Hospital for treatment. It is said that his injuries are very serious.

Girls' Christian Association Fundraising Convention Closes on the 11th

Since the beginning of the Shanghai Girls' Christian Association fundraising convention, with the joint efforts and selfless dedication of the presidents, consultants, captains, and members, the results have been very satisfactory. It is said that the afternoon of December 11th is the closing day of the fundraising convention. The results of each team are being compared with each other, and they all hope to achieve the predetermined goal of 2,000 yuan. Several teams have already exceeded the goal and are competing for the championship in the closing ceremony. In addition to the speech by Mrs. Yu Yingjie, the president of the fundraising committee, as well as the report of the results, awards, and refreshments, a "lighting ceremony" will also be held. The president will award the light to the captains, and the captains will award the light to the members. At that time, the hall will be full of light, which will be a grand occasion. It is said that the slogan of this fundraising convention is "Please come and increase our power to shine." The intention is to hope that the work of the association will rely on the enthusiastic support of consultants and all walks of life, so that it can eliminate darkness and increase light for society. Fire in Zhabei

Rumored to Have Destroyed Japanese Timber

At around 1:50 p.m. yesterday, flames suddenly soared into the sky in the Zhabei area, and thick smoke filled the sky. At that time, it could be seen from the tall buildings in the concession. Afterwards, it was learned that the fire occurred in the area of Yongxing Road and Baoshan Road in Zhabei. However, it was impossible to find out whether the burnt items were houses or other buildings. One said that the fire was caused by timber and goods piled up by the Japanese, but this could not be confirmed. The fire gradually died down at around 2 o'clock.

Fuxing Road Traffic Restored

Barbed Wire Has Been Removed Yesterday

The intersection of the bottom of North Jiangxi Road and Bazi Road was equipped with barbed wire frames and other obstacles during the Shanghai War. When the Japanese army blockaded the eastern section of North Jiangxi Road, another barbed wire frame was added there. The passage from North Jiangxi Road to Fuxing Road was also blocked by barbed wire and other obstacles, and pedestrians had to detour. Until yesterday, several Japanese soldiers carried knives and axes and removed the barbed wire frames placed at the intersection of the bottom of North Jiangxi Road and Bazi Road and at the passage to Fuxing Road. The traffic between North Jiangxi Road and Fuxing Road has now been restored, but the western side of the blocked area of North Jiangxi Road and the eastern section of Bazi Road are still blocked by barbed wire frames.

After the Success of Sino-Soviet Airmail, Shanghai-Europe Airmail Route

After the success of the Chongqing-Moscow air route, airmail to European countries can be sent via this route in the future. However, according to a Datsong News Agency reporter who inquired at the Shanghai Post Office, it is currently more convenient to ship airmail from the city to European countries by boat to Hong Kong, where it is transferred to aircraft for Europe. Therefore, it has not been received and sent via the Sino-Soviet airmail route. However, post offices in Chengdu, Chongqing, Kunming, and Hami have begun to receive and send mail.

Refugee Association Conducts Second Phase of Fundraising

The Shanghai Refugee Relief Association's Citizens Group has sent a letter to the captains of each fundraising team yesterday in order to promote the second phase of fundraising. The letter reads: "Dear Sir/Madam, In accordance with the resolution of the association, this association has adjusted the fundraising team to continue to carry out the fundraising work. We are deeply grateful for your enthusiasm for charity and participation in sponsorship. We are now sending you a copy of the fundraising outline and incentive measures, as well as two books of adoption certificates (please collect them at any time if they are not enough). Please check and receive them, and please also ask for widespread fundraising. According to the organizational outline of the second phase of the fundraising team of the association, the goal is to raise another 100,000 yuan. The lowest target for each team's fundraising is to raise 500 yuan in adoption funds or adopt 100 refugees. The captains of each team are only responsible for fundraising and do not directly receive funds. The fundraising results of each team will be reported and submitted by this association on a regular basis. Each team must fill in a performance report form when reporting the fundraising results, and attach the first copy of the adoption certificate for verification. Incentive regulations: (1) The captain and deputy captain of the fundraising team will be presented with a letter of thanks. (2) Individuals in each team who raise more than 500 yuan in adoption donations will be awarded a medal. (3) Individuals in each team who raise more than 1,000 yuan in adoption donations will be awarded a commemorative mirror frame. (4) Individuals in each team who raise more than 2,000 yuan in adoption donations will be awarded a commemorative plaque. (5) The team with the best overall performance will be rewarded separately."

Christmas Card Posting Schedule to Europe

If Sent by Airmail, It Can Arrive in France Before the Holiday

Recently, as Christmas and the New Year are approaching, foreigners in the city are enthusiastically sending greeting cards. However, due to the war raging in Europe this year, the number of deliveries will inevitably be less than in previous years. On the 3rd of this month, a large batch of greeting card mail was shipped from Shanghai via the Suez Canal to Europe, and will arrive in Marseille on the 28th of this month and in London on the 30th. If sent by airmail, it will be sent from Shanghai to Hong Kong on the 7th of this month, and then transferred to an airplane. It will take off on the 13th and arrive in Paris and Marseille on the 21st of this month, which is just before Christmas and more convenient than before. In addition, a large batch of European mail was sent to Europe via the Pacific Ocean yesterday (the 4th), and is expected to arrive in London on January 10th (1940). On the 11th of this month, another batch will be sent to Europe via the Suez Canal, and will arrive in London on January 13th.

Bizarre Kidnapping Case Occurred on Jiaozhou Road the Night Before Last, Xiao Was Suddenly Kidnapped on the Way Home from the Theater, Watchman Reported to the Police with Suspicious Behavior and Was Detained, and the Suspect Was Arrested Together with the Domestic Servant

At 8:50 p.m. the night before last, a kidnapping case occurred in House No. 11, Lane 148, Jiaozhou Road. The situation is recorded as follows:

Xiao Shi, a Cantonese

He opened the Guangya Dyeing and Weaving Factory at the bottom of Jiaozhou Road and lived with his wife at No. 11, Lane 148, Jiaozhou Road. Yesterday afternoon, Mr. and Mrs. Xiao went out to watch a movie in their own car No. 2477 and returned late at night. After dinner, Xiao went upstairs alone to rest in the bedroom. Unexpectedly, at 8:50 p.m., three kidnappers suddenly entered from the back door, showed guns, and threatened to make a noise. One of the kidnappers went upstairs,

Kidnapped Xiao

Dragged him into a pre-hired car, and drove away quickly. Before leaving, the bandits falsely said that they were sent by the police station, and told them not to be afraid. Unexpectedly, after the kidnappers left, not long after, Wang Jinshan, a watchman from No. 1470 in the lane, who was a native of Anhui, first broke into Xiao's house and reported to the police station by telephone that Xiao had been kidnapped. When the Jing'an Temple Police Station heard the alarm, they immediately sent Chinese detective Wu Wenke and Western detective Gulokov to investigate. Because the kidnappers had just left in this case, the people in the room had not yet reported to the police, but the doorkeeper Wang Jinshan already knew everything,

First Report

This situation was really suspicious, so he asked Wang for information. According to him, before the kidnappers kidnapped Xiao Shi, they first threatened him, took away his gun, and ordered him to face the wall. After the kidnapping, they returned the gun to him. His confession was vague and highly suspicious, so he was arrested and taken to the police station along with Lu Fusheng, a 14-year-old runaway servant from Anhui at Xiao's house. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Jiang Baolian stated the above situation, saying that Chen Fusheng and his brother Chen Yinsheng had been

Adopted and raised by Xiao since childhood

Later, Chen Yinsheng was introduced by someone to work at the Hollywood Casino. Recently, Chen Yinsheng asked Xiao's wife for a loan but failed. He held a grudge and once expressed in front of Wang Jinshan that he wanted to kidnap Xiao. Before the incident last night, Xiao's wife also saw Chen Yinsheng in the lane, so Wang Chen was highly suspected, and he should be allowed to be detained for investigation. After the judge Xiao checked the confession, he ordered that he be allowed to be detained for seven days for further investigation.

The Property of the Sanjiao Leshan Temple Is in Constant Litigation

A temple of the Sanjiao Leshan Temple in Shengdeli, Rue du Pere Froc, French Concession, was mortgaged to the British business Guangdi Real Estate Company by the former abbot. Because it was not redeemed when it was due, the principal and interest totaled 18,000 yuan. Guangdi Company sued the Second Special Court, and the judgment was made to execute the auction. Abbot Qinliang of Jingci Temple in Hangzhou purchased it from Guangdi Company as a branch of Jingci Temple. When taking over, because the current

Abbot Yuanhua

The monks did not want to move out on the orders of the board of directors, Yuanhua filed a lawsuit with the Civil Court of the Second Special Court against Qinliang to confirm the ownership of the temple property, while Qinliang also filed a private prosecution with the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court against Yuanhua for occupying the temple property and obstructing freedom. Yuanhua also filed a counterclaim, and it was discussed that criminal proceedings would be carried out after the civil confirmation of property rights was determined. Later, Monk Guanru, the abbot of Yuhuang Temple adjacent to Sanjiao Leshan Temple (formerly Abbot Yangxi of Jing'an Temple in the West of Shanghai), also filed a private prosecution in the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court against Monk Qinliang for

Obstructing the Freedom of Worship

Qinliang also filed a counterclaim for false accusation. As a result, Qinliang was found not guilty, and Guanru was sentenced to two months' imprisonment with a two-year reprieve. The three parties were constantly litigating for the property of the Sanjiao Leshan Temple. The situation has been recorded in previous reports. Now, Monk Qinliang has filed a complaint with the French Police Station, accusing Monks Guanru and Ziqing of occupying the property of the Sanjiao Leshan Temple, which has made it impossible to take over for a long time since the purchase, and has obstructed freedom. He requested that the case be investigated. The police chief approved the words and summoned the two defendants to the case.

After an Investigation

Yesterday afternoon, the two parties were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. Lawyer Fei Xizhen of the French Concession Administrative Authority explained the case and filed a public prosecution on the charge of obstructing freedom. After Judge Qiu Huanxing questioned the plaintiff Qinliang and the defendants Guanru and Ziqing, he instructed that the hearing be postponed to the 20th for further investigation. After leaving the court, Monk Qinliang also

Incited the Case of Rolling Away

Wan Yuan was arrested and imprisoned and is now serving his sentence, while Sun Lanzhen confessed when she was arrested that she had taken out three gold bracelets and 2,000 yuan in cash when she rolled away, and handed them over to Wan Yuan, who transferred them to Qinliang for the purchase of the property of the Sanjiao Leshan Temple. Yang Yunwu then filed a lawsuit against Qinliang, and the court repeatedly issued summonses, but Qinliang avoided appearing in court. Yesterday, the investigating detective learned that Qinliang had come to court to respond to the case of Guanru and Ziqing obstructing freedom, so he took Qinliang to the police station to await verification.

Embezzlement of Hardware Materials, Civil and Criminal Cases Adjudicated

Fan Dazhang (also known as Fan Juemin), a native of Ningbo, was a broker in Fuxingxiang Hardware Store at No. 263 Chengdu Road. From August 15th to November 9th of this year, Fan suddenly used the names of Taikang Biscuit Company, Tianyi Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Xieji Timber Store, and Guangzhong Paper Mill to privately engrave seals. He used fraudulent methods to embezzle 9,038 yuan of hardware materials. Xie Shaofang, the owner of Fuxingxiang Store, found out and hired Lawyer Le Junwei to report to the police station, ordering the detectives to arrest Fan Dazhang and escort him to the First Special Court. After repeated interrogations, the case has been concluded. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao announced the verdict in the Second Criminal Court. Fan Dazhang was sentenced to one year and two months' imprisonment for continuous embezzlement of business property. In the attached civil lawsuit, Fan Dazhang should repay the plaintiff 5,783 yuan and 6 jiao and 5 fen. If he is still unable to repay after compulsory execution, his guarantor Pu Meisheng shall be responsible for compensation. The forged receipts, return receipts, and seals shall be confiscated as listed.

Impersonating and Claiming Remittances, Bailer to be Summoned for Further Interrogation

Chen Qianwen, a 17-year-old girl from Guangdong, residing at No. 32, Jiande Lane, Yuyuan Road, entrusted Ugo Cheiso, an Italian who had dealings with Citibank on Jiujiang Road, to guarantee between October 18th and last month, impersonating and claiming 1,800 US dollars (more than 20,000 legal currency) remitted from San Francisco, USA to Shanghai and delivered to Chen Sanmei. At the end of last month, Chen Sanmei, who resided at No. 4, Jing'an Villa, took a letter to the bank to question why the funds remitted from San Francisco had not been notified for collection for so long. At this point, the bank realized the mistake, so it secretly sent someone to the address to arrest Chen Qianwen and hand her over to the police station for escort to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention for investigation. The defendant claimed that she had an uncle doing business in San Francisco. When Citibank notified her to collect the funds last month, the name translated by the English translator was similar to her name. She thought it was the funds sent by her uncle and did not intend to defraud. The case was continued yesterday morning, and the police station filed a public prosecution against the defendant for fraud. Judge Zhan presided over the trial. The police station requested an extension because the Italian who guaranteed the collection of funds sent a telegram from Tokyo stating that he would return to Shanghai within three or four days to testify in court. The court checked the words and ordered the defendant to be remanded and the trial adjourned.

According to Japanese sources, Ge Shusen, a certain team leader from Hebei who was assassinated on Foch Road the day before yesterday, hired a car himself after the incident and went to Fumin Hospital on North Sichuan Road for treatment because Ge was shot in the leg during the assassination. At around 10 a.m. the day before yesterday, a shooting incident occurred at the intersection of Foch Road and Weihaiwei Road, the boundary between the British and French concessions. Ge Shusen, the person who was shot, dodged quickly when he heard the gunshot and fell to the ground, thus escaping the disaster. At that time, three pedestrians were injured and two were killed by stray bullets, and the shooter was finally arrested. The details have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. According to the reporter of Huawen News Agency, the reason for this shooting is that Ge's nickname is Ah San, he is 50 years old, a native of Hebei Province, illiterate, and very burly. He used to serve as an inspector in the Municipal Police Bureau. Recently, a certain party commissioned him to organize the "Special Service Third Brigade." Ge did his best to flatter him, so he was valued by his superiors. Ge acted as an accomplice to the tiger and summoned bandits to join the team in the name of expanding the team, but they had to bring guns and equipment with them. When the guns and equipment were in hand, they were disbanded. Those who resisted were subjected to various tortures. Therefore, many people were fooled, so they were extremely resentful and came up with this strategy to avenge themselves.

Zhang Deqing, the Owner of Huanhua Iron Factory, Was Kidnapped Yesterday and Was Taken Away by Two Female Bandits in a Car and Disappeared

Huanhua Iron Factory is located at No. 364, Lane 1125, Yuyuan Road. The owner of the factory is named Zhang Deqing. The factory has a very thick capital and a considerable scale. Zhang's residence is in the French Concession. He must go to the factory every morning to work, and occasionally return home for lunch. Yesterday around noon at 12 o'clock, when Zhang was clearing debts in the factory and preparing lunch, more than a dozen male and female bandits suddenly rushed in with weapons and broke into Zhang's office. First, they drove and imprisoned all the staff in the room, and then two female bandits took out pistols and forced Zhang Deqing to follow them. Zhang had no choice but to let them do as they pleased. At that time, the two female bandits held Zhang on the left and right, went to the front of the factory gate, and made him enter a car parked on the side of the road and left. Afterwards, the factory urgently reported to the police station for assistance.
